    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">April 30,
2010</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Dear
Shareholder and/or Friend of Zion...</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">During
the past two weeks, Israel celebrated its 62<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">nd</font>
birthday and, almost to the day, Zion Oil &amp; Gas celebrated its 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">th</font>
birthday.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">According
to Harvard University Professor of Economic History, David Landes, &#8220;In the last
50 years, only one country in the world has moved from being a third world
economy to a first world economy&#8230;and that is Israel!&#8221;</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">At Zion
Oil, we believe that we may be able to help Israel's economy (soon, we hope) by
discovering significant quantities of oil and gas onshore in
Israel.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We are
not completely alone in our belief that there are significant quantities of oil
and gas waiting to be discovered. You can read below the latest estimates of the
United States Department of the Interior (Geological Survey Department) and also
the thoughts of Hal Lindsey in his recent weekly report.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In any
event, our daily efforts continue steadily and with determined focus. So, here
is the report of Zion&#8217;s work during the past two weeks:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Rights
Offering</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On April
26, 2010, we announced (click here to read the press release) that we will soon
be launching a rights offering.&#160;&#160;On April 28, 2010, we filed our
prospectus supplement, including the details of the offering. Under the rights
offering, holders of Zion&#8217;s stock at the close of business on May 6, 2010 (the
Record Date) will be issued, at no charge, one subscription right for every two
shares of stock owned.&#160;&#160;Each subscription right will entitle the
holder to purchase one share of Zion stock at a price of $5.00, irrespective of
the market price.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This
rights offering is utilizing our effective shelf registration statement on Form
S-3 and the subscription rights may be exercised at any time prior to 5:00 pm
EDT on June 30, 2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As soon
as practicable, after May 6, 2010, we will mail to our stockholders a prospectus
and other items necessary for exercising the rights.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As noted
in the press release, we plan to use the proceeds from the rights offering: (a)
to purchase a 51% interest in a new company (Zion Drilling, Inc. that will own a
2,000 horsepower drilling rig), (b) to drill further 'deep' exploration wells on
Zion's licenses in Israel (in continuation of Zion's oil and gas exploration
efforts) and (c) for general corporate purposes.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><IMG SRC="pic1.jpg"></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><IMG SRC="pic2.jpg"></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Meetings
in Ankara, Turkey</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Memorandum of Understanding
(MoU) with Aladdin Middle East, Ltd. (AME)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This past
week, as you can see in the photographs, I visited AME&#8217;s offices in Ankara,
Turkey, in order to sign original copies of the MoU and discuss in detail Zion&#8217;s
plans for future drilling onshore Israel.&#160;&#160;The press release regarding
the MoU was issued on April 19, 2010 and detailed our plans to secure the 2,000
horsepower drilling rig in Israel on a permanent basis (click here to read the
press release).</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">I&#8217;m
pleased to report that my meetings with AME were both agreeable and
productive.&#160;&#160;We signed the original MoU copies and will move forward
just as fast as we can.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Personally,
I have found AME&#8217;s management, administrative staff, and drilling personnel to
be courteous, professional and a pleasure to work with.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The United States Geological
Survey (USGS Survey)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On April
8, 2010, the USGS issued a report with the title: &#8220;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">Assessment of
Undiscovered Oil and Gas Resources of the Levant Basin Province, Eastern
Mediterranean</font>.&#8221;&#160;&#160;You can review the USGS Survey by clicking
here.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The USGS
Survey estimates a mean of 1.7 <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">BILLION</font> barrels of
recoverable oil and 122 <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">TRILLION</font> cubic feet
of recoverable gas in the Levant Basin. I note that all of Zion&#8217;s exploration
areas fall within the Levant Basin.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">I'll also
note that the USGS Survey cites seven references and three of those references
were co-authored by Zion director (and Chairman of Zion&#8217;s Technical Committee)
Dr. Druckman (who is also Israel&#8217;s previous Petroleum
Commissioner).</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">At
today&#8217;s prices (see www.oil-price.net), the value of the undiscovered oil and
gas assessed in the USGS Survey amounts to approximately $650 Billion US
Dollars... By any measure, that's a very large financial treasure waiting to be
discovered.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Hal Lindsey
Report</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On April
23, 2010, Hal Lindsey published his weekly report on the Internet.&#160;&#160;At
approximately 18 minutes into the report he commented on oil and gas in Israel,
the USGS Survey, Noble Energy and Zion Oil &amp; Gas.&#160;&#160;You may be
interested to view the report here &#8211; we certainly appreciate Hal Lindsey&#8217;s
support.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">With
regard to 'Operations', we are now preparing for the next well, as you can
read.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma&#8217;anit-Rehoboth #2
Well</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Following
completion of production testing operations, this well was temporarily suspended
for possible future use as an offset well to the Ma&#8217;anit-Joseph #3 (M-J #3) well
(see below) which is to be drilled a short distance away.&#160;&#160;The
drilling rig is currently being secured &#8216;on-site&#8217; and undergoing maintenance,
until it is called into service to spud the M-J #3 well in the near
future.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma&#8217;anit-Joseph #3 Well (M-J
#3)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Further
to our ongoing exploration work on the Ma&#8217;anit geological structure, we are
moving forward with permitting for the M-J #3 well.&#160;&#160;This past week we
met with Kibbutz Ma&#8217;anit in order to discuss terms for drilling the M-J #3 well
on their land, not far from the site of the previous well, the Ma&#8217;anit-Rehoboth
#2 well.&#160;&#160;I&#8217;m pleased to report that our meeting was most
amicable.&#160;&#160;This new well is targeted at the (&#8220;deep&#8221;) Permian
geological layer and we estimate that we will &#8220;spud&#8221; (i.e. begin drilling) the
well in the summer of 2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Elijah #3
Well</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As
previously reported, the Elijah #3 well was drilled to a depth of approximately
10,938 feet (3,334 meters) when the drill string became stuck within the Asher
Volcanics section of the hole. After recovering a significant portion of the
stuck drill pipe, progress in recovering the remainder of the pipe slowed and
the decision was made to temporarily suspend drilling operations pending further
analysis of the situation.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We have
now decided to acquire some additional field seismic data that will help us to
resolve certain questions regarding the geology of the area surrounding the
Elijah #3 well. The timing for this work is scheduled to take place in
mid-summer 2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The
Issachar-Zebulun Permit Area</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Zion and
the Geophysical Institute of Israel (GII) have signed an agreement for GII, on
behalf of Zion, to acquire approximately 30 kilometers of seismic data in Zion&#8217;s
Issachar-Zebulun Permit area. The timing for the field work is scheduled to
coincide with the seismic field work for the Elijah #3 project
area.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

Stockholders</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
annual meeting is scheduled to take place at the Dan Caesarea Hotel in Caesarea,
Israel at 2:00 p.m. (local time) on Monday June 14, 2010.&#160;&#160;If you are
planning to attend the meeting in person and would like to reserve a room at the
Dan Caesarea Hotel, please contact Ora Weisman in our Israel office at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">ora@zionoil.com</font> to
take advantage of a special room rate offered only to Zion
shareholders.</font></div>

prior years, the SEC allowed brokers to vote the shares of stockholders who held
shares at the broker but did not express an opinion regarding how they wished to
vote their shares.&#160;&#160;The new rules do not allow your shares to be voted
on certain items without you personally voting your shares, so <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">please
vote your shares</font>.</font></div>
